**ุงูฺฏู ณ: ูููุฏุงุฑ ุฒูุงู (Timeline)**

```latex
\begin{figure}[htbp]
    \centering
    \begin{tikzpicture}[
        phase/.style={
            draw, rounded corners, minimum height=1.5cm, 
            minimum width=3cm, align=center, font=\small\bfseries
        }
    ]

    \draw[ultra thick, -Stealth, gray] (0,0) -- (16,0);
    
    % ูุงุฒูุง
    \node[phase, fill=ActionYellow!30] at (1.5,1.5) {ูพุดโฺฏุฐุงุฑ\\ฑฒ-ถ ูุงู};
    \node[phase, fill=RiskRed!30] at (4.5,1.5) {ูุงุฒ ฑ\\ุชุซุจุช\\ูุงู ฑ-ถ};
    \node[phase, fill=ScenarioOrange!30] at (8,1.5) {ูุงุฒ ฒ\\ููุงุฏุณุงุฒ\\ูุงู ถ-ฒด};
    \node[phase, fill=CompareGreen!30] at (11.5,1.5) {ูุงุฒ ณ\\ุชุญฺฉู\\ูุงู ฒด-ถฐ};
    \node[phase, fill=TheoryBlue!30] at (14.5,1.5) {ูุงุฒ ด\\ูพโฺฏุฑ\\ูุงู ถฐ+};
    
    % ูุดุงูฺฏุฑูุง ุฒูุงู
    \foreach \x/\t in {0/ุดุฑูุน, 3/ูุงู ถ, 6/ุณุงู ฑ, 9/ุณุงู ฒ, 12/ุณุงู ต, 15/ุณุงู ฑฐ} {
        \draw[thick] (\x,0.2) -- (\x,-0.2) node[below, font=\tiny] {\t};
    }
    
    \end{tikzpicture}
    \caption{ุฌุฏูู ุฒูุงู ูุงุฒุจูุฏ ูุธุงุฑุช ุจูโุงูููู}
    \label{fig:timeline}
\end{figure}
```

### ณ.ฒ ุงูฺฏู ุงูู ุฌุฏูู

```latex

### ถ.ณ ุงูฺฏููุง LaTeX ุจุฑุง ุบูโุณุงุฒ ุจุตุฑ

**ุตูุญูโ ุชุชุฑุงฺ ูุตู:**

```latex
% ============================================
% ุตูุญูโ ุขุบุงุฒู ูุตู (Chapter Opening)
% ============================================

\newcommand{\chapteropening}[4]{%
    % #1 = ุดูุงุฑู ูุตู
    % #2 = ุนููุงู ูุตู
    % #3 = ุฑูฺฏ ูุตู
    % #4 = ูููโููู
    \clearpage
    \thispagestyle{empty}
    \begin{tikzpicture}[remember picture, overlay]
        % ูพุณโุฒููู ุฑูฺฏ
        \fill[#3!15] 
            (current page.south west) rectangle 
            (current page.north east);
        
        % ููุงุฑ ุฑูฺฏ ุจุงูุง
        \fill[#3] 
            ([yshift=-3cm]current page.north west) rectangle 
            (current page.north east);
        
        % ุดูุงุฑู ูุตู (ุจุฒุฑฺฏ)
        \node[
            anchor=north east,
            font=\fontsize{80}{80}\selectfont\bfseries,
            text=#3!30
        ] at ([xshift=-2cm, yshift=-1cm]current page.north east) 
            {#1};
        
        % ุนููุงู ูุตู
        \node[
            anchor=center,
            font=\Huge\bfseries,
            text=white
        ] at ([yshift=-1.5cm]current page.north) 
            {#2};
        
        % ุฎุท ุฌุฏุงฺฉููุฏู
        \draw[#3, ultra thick] 
            ([yshift=-4cm, xshift=3cm]current page.north west) -- 
            ([yshift=-4cm, xshift=-3cm]current page.north east);
        
        % ูููโููู
        \node[
            anchor=center,
            text width=12cm,
            align=center,
            font=\large\itshape,
            text=#3!80!black
        ] at ([yshift=-2cm]current page.center) 
            {ยซ#4ยป};
        
    \end{tikzpicture}
    \clearpage
}

% ---- ุงุณุชูุงุฏู ----
\chapteropening{ณ}{ุฑูฺฉุฑุฏูุง ู ุณุงุฎุชุงุฑูุง ูุธุงุฑุช}{CompareGreen}{%
    ุฏููฺฉุฑุงุณ ฺุฒ ูุณุช ฺฉู ฺฉโุจุงุฑ ุจู ุฏุณุช ุขุฏ ู ุจุฑุง ููุดู ุจูุงูุฏุ 
    ุจุงุฏ ูุฑ ุฑูุฒ ุงุฒ ูู ุชููุฏุด ุฏุงุฏ. โ ูุงุชุณูุงู ูุงูู
}
```

**ูููุฏุงุฑ ุฏุฑุฎุช ุชุตูู:**

    boxrule=0.6pt,
    left=6mm,
    right=6mm,
    before skip=10pt,
    after skip=10pt,
    #1
}

% ============================================================
% ฺฉุงุฏุฑ ฑฒ: ูพุฑุณุด ุชุฃูู (Reflection Question)
% ============================================================
\newtcolorbox{reflectionbox}[1][]{
    enhanced,
    breakable,
    colback=PurpleBG,
    colframe=MainPurple!50,
    boxrule=0.4pt,
    borderline south={2pt}{0pt}{MainPurple},
    left=6mm,
    right=6mm,
    top=4mm,
    bottom=4mm,
    before skip=10pt,
    after skip=10pt,
    overlay={
        \node[
            anchor=north west,
            font=\Large,
            text=MainPurple!40
        ] at ([xshift=3mm, yshift=-3mm]frame.north west) {\faQuestion};
    },
    #1
}

% ============================================================
% ฺฉุงุฏุฑ ฑณ: ุขูุงุฑ ู ุงุฑูุงู (Statistics)
% ============================================================
\newtcolorbox{statsbox}[1][]{
    enhanced,
    colback=white,
    colframe=MainBlue,
    boxrule=1.5pt,
    arc=0pt,
    left=6mm,
    right=6mm,
    top=6mm,
    bottom=6mm,
    before skip=10pt,
    after skip=10pt,
    overlay={
        \fill[MainBlue] 
            ([xshift=0pt]frame.north west) rectangle 
            ([xshift=5mm]frame.south west);
        \node[
            anchor=center,
            font=\Large,
            text=white,
            rotate=90
        ] at ([xshift=2.5mm]frame.west) {\faChartBar};
    },
    left=12mm,
    #1
}

% ============================================================
% ฺฉุงุฏุฑ ฑด: ุฎูุงุตูโ ูุตู (ูพุงุงู ูุตู)
% ============================================================
\newtcolorbox{chaptersummary}{
    enhanced,
    breakable,
    colback=VeryLightGray,
    colframe=DarkGray,
    coltitle=white,
    colbacktitle=DarkGray,
    fonttitle=\large\bfseries,
    title={\faListAlt\hspace{8pt}ุฎูุงุตูโ ูุตู},
    arc=3mm,
    boxrule=0.8pt,
    left=8mm,
    right=8mm,
    top=6mm,
    bottom=6mm,
    before skip=20pt,
    after skip=15pt,
    shadow={1mm}{-1mm}{0mm}{black!15}
}

% ============================================================
% ฺฉุงุฏุฑ ฑต: ุงุฑุฌุงุน ุจู ูุตู ุฏฺฏุฑ (Cross-Reference)
% ============================================================
\newtcolorbox{crossref}[1][]{
    enhanced,
    colback=LightPurple!30,
    colframe=MainPurple!30,
    boxrule=0.3pt,
    arc=1mm,
    left=4mm,
    right=4mm,
    top=2mm,
    bottom=2mm,
    before skip=6pt,
    after skip=6pt,
    fontupper=\small,
    overlay={
        \node[
            anchor=west,
            font=\small,
            text=MainPurple
        ] at ([xshift=2mm]frame.west) {\faArrowLeft};
    },
    left=8mm,
    #1
}
```

    % #1 = ุดูุงุฑู ูุตู
    % #2 = ุนููุงู ูุตู
    % #3 = ุฑูฺฏ ูุตู (MainPurple, MainBlue, etc.)
    % #4 = ูููโููู
    % #5 = ููุจุน ูููโููู

    \thispagestyle{empty}
    \begin{tikzpicture}[remember picture, overlay]
        % ูพุณโุฒููู

            (current page.south west) rectangle 
            (current page.north east);
        
        % ููุงุฑ ุจุงูุง

            ([yshift=-4cm]current page.north west) rectangle 
            (current page.north east);
        
        % ุดูุงุฑู ูุตู ุจุฒุฑฺฏ
        \node[
            anchor=north east,
            font=\fontsize{120}{120}\selectfont\bfseries,
            text=#3!20
        ] at ([xshift=-1.5cm, yshift=-0.5cm]current page.north east) 
            {#1};
        
        % ยซูุตูยป
        \node[
            anchor=north west,
            font=\LARGE,
            text=white!80
        ] at ([xshift=2cm, yshift=-1cm]current page.north west) 
            {ูุตู};
        
        % ุนููุงู ูุตู
        \node[
            anchor=north west,
            font=\fontsize{28}{34}\selectfont\bfseries,
            text=white,
            text width=14cm
        ] at ([xshift=2cm, yshift=-2cm]current page.north west) 
            {#2};
        
        % ุฎุท ุชุฒุฆู
        \draw[white, line width=2pt] 
            ([yshift=-4.3cm, xshift=2cm]current page.north west) -- 
            ([yshift=-4.3cm, xshift=8cm]current page.north west);
        
        % ูููโููู

            anchor=center,

        ] at ([yshift=1cm]current page.center) 
            {ยซ#4ยป};
        
        % ููุจุน ูููโููู

            anchor=center,
            font=\normalsize,
            text=#3!50!black

            (current page.south west) rectangle 
            ([yshift=0.5cm]current page.south east);
        
    \end{tikzpicture}
    \clearpage
}

## ูุงู ต: `preamble/layout.tex` โ ุตูุญูโุขุฑุง

```latex
% โโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโ
% โ  ุชูุธูุงุช ุตูุญูโุขุฑุง                                             โ
% โโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโ

% ============================================================
% ุณุฑุตูุญู ู ูพุงุตูุญู
% ============================================================

\pagestyle{fancy}
\fancyhf{}                         % ูพุงฺฉโุณุงุฒ

% ุตูุญุงุช ูุฑุฏ (ุฑุงุณุช)
\fancyhead[RO]{%
    \textcolor{MediumGray}{\small\leftmark}%
}
\fancyhead[LO]{%
    \textcolor{MediumGray}{\small\thepage}%
}

% ุตูุญุงุช ุฒูุฌ (ฺูพ)
\fancyhead[LE]{%
    \textcolor{MediumGray}{\small\thepage}%
}
\fancyhead[RE]{%
    \textcolor{MediumGray}{\small\rightmark}%
}

% ุฎุท ุณุฑุตูุญู
\renewcommand{\headrulewidth}{0.4pt}
\renewcommand{\headrule}{%
    \textcolor{MainPurple!30}{\hrule width\headwidth height\headrulewidth}
}

% ูพุงุตูุญู
\fancyfoot[C]{%
    \textcolor{LightGray}{\rule{4cm}{0.3pt}}\\[-2pt]
    \textcolor{MediumGray}{\footnotesize 
        ูุธุงุฑุช ุจูโุงูููู ุจุฑ ฺฏุฐุงุฑ ุฏููฺฉุฑุงุชฺฉ ุงุฑุงู โ ููุฏ ุณุงูู
    }
}

% ุตูุญุงุช ุขุบุงุฒ ูุตู
\fancypagestyle{plain}{
    \fancyhf{}
    \fancyfoot[C]{\textcolor{MediumGray}{\thepage}}
    \renewcommand{\headrulewidth}{0pt}
}

% ============================================================
% ุนููุงูโุจูุฏ ูุตูู
% ============================================================

% --- ูุตู ---
\titleformat{\chapter}[display]
    {\normalfont\huge\bfseries}
    {}          % ุญุฐู ยซูุตู ฑยป ุฎูุฏฺฉุงุฑ โ ุงุฒ chapteropening ุงุณุชูุงุฏู ูโุดูุฏ
    {0pt}
    {\color{MainPurple}\Huge}
\titlespacing*{\chapter}{0pt}{-30pt}{20pt}

% --- ุจุฎุด ---
\titleformat{\section}
    {\normalfont\Large\bfseries\color{MainBlue}}
    {\thesection}
    {1em}
    {}
    [\vspace{-4pt}\textcolor{MainBlue!30}{\rule{\textwidth}{0.5pt}}]
\titlespacing*{\section}{0pt}{20pt}{10pt}

% --- ุฒุฑุจุฎุด ---
\titleformat{\subsection}
    {\normalfont\large\bfseries\color{MainGreen!80!black}}
    {\thesubsection}
    {1em}
    {}
\titlespacing*{\subsection}{0pt}{15pt}{8pt}

% --- ุฒุฑุฒุฑุจุฎุด ---
\titleformat{\subsubsection}
    {\normalfont\normalsize\bfseries\color{MainOrange!80!black}}
    {\thesubsubsection}
    {1em}
    {}
\titlespacing*{\subsubsection}{0pt}{12pt}{6pt}

% --- ูพุงุฑุงฺฏุฑุงู ---
\titleformat{\paragraph}[runin]
    {\normalfont\normalsize\bfseries\color{DarkGray}}
    {\theparagraph}
    {1em}
    {}
    [.]
\titlespacing*{\paragraph}{0pt}{8pt}{6pt}

% ============================================================
% ููุฑุณุช ูุทุงูุจ
% ============================================================

% ุนูู ุดูุงุฑูโฺฏุฐุงุฑ
\setcounter{secnumdepth}{3}
\setcounter{tocdepth}{2}

% ============================================================
% Epigraph (ูููโููู ุงุจุชุฏุง ูุตู)
% ============================================================
\setlength{\epigraphwidth}{0.7\textwidth}
\setlength{\epigraphrule}{0pt}

% ============================================================
% ุนููุงูโูุง ูุงุฑุณ
% ============================================================
% (ูพุณ ุงุฒ ุจุงุฑฺฏุฐุงุฑ xepersian ุฏุฑ main.tex ุชุนุฑู ุฎูุงููุฏ ุดุฏ)
```

\section{ูฺฉุงุชุจ ูฺฉุฑ ูุทุงูุนุงุช ฺฏุฐุงุฑ}

\begin{recommendation}
\textbf{ุจุฑุง ุงุฑุงู:}

\subsection{ูุญุฏูุฏู ู ูฺฉุงูุฒูโูุง}

## ุงุณฺฉุฑูพุช PowerShell: ุณุงุฎุช ุณุงุฎุชุงุฑ ูุงูโูุง

ุงุณฺฉุฑูพุช ุฒุฑ ุฑุง ุฏุฑ PowerShell ุงุฌุฑุง ฺฉูุฏ. ุชูุงู ูพูุดูโูุง ู ูุงูโูุง ุณุงุฎุชู ูโุดููุฏ:

```powershell
# ============================================================
# ุณุงุฎุช ุณุงุฎุชุงุฑ ูพุฑูฺู ฺฉุชุงุจ
# ูุธุงุฑุช ุจูโุงูููู ุจุฑ ฺฏุฐุงุฑ ุฏููฺฉุฑุงุชฺฉ ุงุฑุงู
# ============================================================

$root = "iran-transition-monitoring"

# ุณุงุฎุช ูพูุดูโูุง
$dirs = @(
    "$root",
    "$root/preamble",
    "$root/chapters",
    "$root/appendices",
    "$root/figures",
    "$root/figures/diagrams",
    "$root/figures/charts",
    "$root/figures/maps",
    "$root/figures/photos",
    "$root/figures/logos",
    "$root/figures/infographics",
    "$root/figures/icons",
    "$root/tables",
    "$root/fonts",
    "$root/output"
)

foreach ($d in $dirs) {
    New-Item -ItemType Directory -Path $d -Force | Out-Null
    Write-Host "DIR  $d" -ForegroundColor Green
}

# ูุงูโูุง preamble
$preambleFiles = @(
    "packages.tex",
    "colors.tex",
    "boxes.tex",
    "commands.tex",
    "layout.tex",
    "fonts.tex"
)

foreach ($f in $preambleFiles) {
    $path = "$root/preamble/$f"
    if (-not (Test-Path $path)) {
        New-Item -ItemType File -Path $path -Force | Out-Null
    }
    Write-Host "FILE $path" -ForegroundColor Cyan
}

# ูุงูโูุง chapters
$chapterFiles = @(
    "titlepage.tex",
    "dedication.tex",
    "ch00-preface.tex",
    "ch01-theoretical.tex",
    "ch02-why-iran.tex",
    "ch03-approaches.tex",
    "ch04-scenarios.tex",
    "ch05-actors.tex",
    "ch06-guarantees.tex",
    "ch07-risks.tex",
    "ch08-requirements.tex",
    "ch09-timeline.tex",
    "ch10-budget.tex",
    "ch11-roadmap.tex",
    "ch12-conclusion.tex"
)

foreach ($f in $chapterFiles) {
    $path = "$root/chapters/$f"
    if (-not (Test-Path $path)) {
        New-Item -ItemType File -Path $path -Force | Out-Null
    }
    Write-Host "FILE $path" -ForegroundColor Yellow
}

# ูุงูโูุง appendices
$appendixFiles = @(
    "app-A-comparison.tex",
    "app-B-south-africa.tex",
    "app-C-chile.tex",
    "app-D-tunisia.tex",
    "app-E-poland.tex",
    "app-F-iraq.tex",
    "app-G-myanmar.tex",
    "app-H-timor.tex",
    "app-I-glossary.tex",
    "app-J-directory.tex"
)

foreach ($f in $appendixFiles) {
    $path = "$root/appendices/$f"
    if (-not (Test-Path $path)) {
        New-Item -ItemType File -Path $path -Force | Out-Null
    }
    Write-Host "FILE $path" -ForegroundColor Magenta
}

# ูุงูโูุง ุฑุดู
$rootFiles = @(
    "main.tex",
    "references.bib",
    "glossary.tex"
)

foreach ($f in $rootFiles) {
    $path = "$root/$f"
    if (-not (Test-Path $path)) {
        New-Item -ItemType File -Path $path -Force | Out-Null
    }
    Write-Host "FILE $path" -ForegroundColor White
}

# ุณุงุฎุช ูุงู references.bib ุจุง ูุญุชูุง ุงููู
$bibContent = @'
% ============================================================

# ุณุงุฎุช ุงุณฺฉุฑูพุช ฺฉุงููพุงู
$buildScript = @'
#!/bin/bash
echo "=== Compiling: Iran Democratic Transition Monitoring ==="
echo "Step 1: First XeLaTeX pass..."
xelatex main.tex
echo "Step 2: Biber (bibliography)..."
biber main
echo "Step 3: Glossaries..."
makeglossaries main
echo "Step 4: Second XeLaTeX pass..."
xelatex main.tex
echo "Step 5: Third XeLaTeX pass..."
xelatex main.tex
echo "Step 6: Moving output..."
cp main.pdf output/
echo "=== Done! Output: output/main.pdf ==="
grep -c "Warning" main.log
echo " warnings found (see main.log)"
'@

Set-Content -Path "$root/build.sh" -Value $buildScript -Encoding UTF8
Write-Host "build.sh created" -ForegroundColor Green

# ุงุณฺฉุฑูพุช ฺฉุงููพุงู ููุฏูุฒ
$buildPS = @'
Write-Host "=== Compiling: Iran Democratic Transition Monitoring ===" -ForegroundColor Cyan
Write-Host "Step 1: First XeLaTeX pass..."
xelatex main.tex
Write-Host "Step 2: Biber (bibliography)..."
biber main
Write-Host "Step 3: Glossaries..."
makeglossaries main
Write-Host "Step 4: Second XeLaTeX pass..."
xelatex main.tex
Write-Host "Step 5: Third XeLaTeX pass..."
xelatex main.tex
Write-Host "Step 6: Moving output..."
Copy-Item main.pdf output/ -Force
Write-Host "=== Done! Output: output/main.pdf ===" -ForegroundColor Green
$warnings = (Select-String -Path main.log -Pattern "Warning" | Measure-Object).Count
Write-Host "$warnings warnings found (see main.log)" -ForegroundColor Yellow
'@

Set-Content -Path "$root/build.ps1" -Value $buildPS -Encoding UTF8
Write-Host "build.ps1 created" -ForegroundColor Green

# ุฎูุงุตู
Write-Host "`n============================================" -ForegroundColor Cyan
Write-Host "  Project structure created successfully!" -ForegroundColor Green
Write-Host "  Root: $root" -ForegroundColor White
Write-Host "============================================" -ForegroundColor Cyan

$totalDirs = (Get-ChildItem -Path $root -Directory -Recurse).Count
$totalFiles = (Get-ChildItem -Path $root -File -Recurse).Count
Write-Host "  Directories: $totalDirs" -ForegroundColor Green
Write-Host "  Files: $totalFiles" -ForegroundColor Yellow
Write-Host "============================================`n" -ForegroundColor Cyan

Write-Host "Next steps:" -ForegroundColor White
Write-Host "  1. Copy preamble content into preamble/*.tex files" -ForegroundColor Gray
Write-Host "  2. Copy chapter content into chapters/*.tex files" -ForegroundColor Gray
Write-Host "  3. Copy main.tex content" -ForegroundColor Gray
Write-Host "  4. Install fonts (XB Zar or Vazirmatn)" -ForegroundColor Gray
Write-Host "  5. Run: cd $root; .\build.ps1" -ForegroundColor Gray
```

## ุงุณฺฉุฑูพุช ุชุฃุฏ ุณุงุฎุชุงุฑ

ูพุณ ุงุฒ ุงุฌุฑุง ุงุณฺฉุฑูพุช ุจุงูุงุ ุจุฑุง ุชุฃุฏ ุงูฺฉู ููู ฺุฒ ุฏุฑุณุช ุณุงุฎุชู ุดุฏู:

```powershell
# ุชุฃุฏ ุณุงุฎุชุงุฑ
$root = "iran-transition-monitoring"

Write-Host "`n=== Verifying Project Structure ===" -ForegroundColor Cyan

# ุจุฑุฑุณ ูพูุดูโูุง
$expectedDirs = @(
    "preamble", "chapters", "appendices",
    "figures", "figures/diagrams", "figures/charts",
    "figures/maps", "figures/photos", "figures/logos",
    "figures/infographics", "figures/icons",
    "tables", "fonts", "output"
)

$missingDirs = 0
foreach ($d in $expectedDirs) {
    $path = "$root/$d"
    if (Test-Path $path) {
        Write-Host "  [OK] $d" -ForegroundColor Green
    } else {
        Write-Host "  [MISSING] $d" -ForegroundColor Red
        $missingDirs++
    }
}

# ุจุฑุฑุณ ูุงูโูุง ฺฉูุฏ
$expectedFiles = @(
    "main.tex", "references.bib", "glossary.tex",
    "README.md", "build.ps1", ".gitignore",
    "preamble/packages.tex", "preamble/boxes.tex",
    "preamble/commands.tex", "preamble/layout.tex",
    "preamble/fonts.tex",
    "chapters/titlepage.tex", "chapters/dedication.tex",
    "chapters/ch00-preface.tex", "chapters/ch01-theoretical.tex",
    "chapters/ch02-why-iran.tex", "chapters/ch03-approaches.tex",
    "chapters/ch04-scenarios.tex", "chapters/ch05-actors.tex",
    "chapters/ch06-guarantees.tex", "chapters/ch07-risks.tex",
    "chapters/ch08-requirements.tex", "chapters/ch09-timeline.tex",
    "chapters/ch10-budget.tex", "chapters/ch11-roadmap.tex",
    "chapters/ch12-conclusion.tex"
)

$missingFiles = 0
foreach ($f in $expectedFiles) {
    $path = "$root/$f"
    if (Test-Path $path) {
        $size = (Get-Item $path).Length
        if ($size -gt 0) {
            Write-Host "  [OK] $f ($size bytes)" -ForegroundColor Green
        } else {
            Write-Host "  [EMPTY] $f" -ForegroundColor Yellow
        }
    } else {
        Write-Host "  [MISSING] $f" -ForegroundColor Red
        $missingFiles++
    }
}

Write-Host "`n=== Summary ===" -ForegroundColor Cyan
if ($missingDirs -eq 0 -and $missingFiles -eq 0) {
    Write-Host "  All directories and files present!" -ForegroundColor Green
} else {
    Write-Host "  Missing dirs: $missingDirs | Missing files: $missingFiles" -ForegroundColor Red
}
```

## ูุงู `chapters/ch04-scenarios.tex` โ ุจุฎุด ุงูู

```latex
% โโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโโ

\begin{operationalnote}

\begin{lessonlearned}
